 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 1.01 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>MICROSOFT CORPORATION </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>CONFLICT MINERALS
REPORT </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>FOR THE REPORTING PERIOD FROM </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>JANUARY&nbsp;1 TO DECEMBER&nbsp;31, 2016 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>I.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>INTRODUCTION </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">This Conflict Minerals Report (&#147;CMR&#148;) for MICROSOFT CORPORATION is filed as an exhibit to
Microsoft&#146;s Form SD pursuant to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">13p-1</FONT> under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 (the &#147;Rule&#148;) for the 2016 reporting year. The report covers all Microsoft majority-owned subsidiaries and
variable interest entities that are subject to the Rule (&#147;Microsoft&#148;). The Rule imposes certain due diligence and reporting obligations on US Securities and Exchange Commission (&#147;SEC&#148;) registrants whose manufactured products
(including products contracted to be made for each registrant) contain &#147;conflict minerals&#148; necessary to the functionality or production of those products. The Rule defines &#147;conflict minerals&#148; to include cassiterite,
columbite-tantalite, gold, wolframite and their derivatives limited to tin, tantalum, tungsten, and gold (collectively referred to as &#147;3TGs&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft
develops, licenses, and supports a wide range of software products, services, and hardware devices (&#147;devices&#148;) that deliver new opportunities, greater convenience, and enhanced value to people&#146;s lives. Microsoft is committed to the
responsible sourcing of raw materials globally in support of human rights, labor, health and safety, environmental protection, and business ethics. Our commitment and strategy are outlined in Microsoft&#146;s <FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Responsible Sourcing of Raw Materials</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;RSRM&#148;) policy. Under our policy, Microsoft takes a holistic approach to the responsible sourcing of raw
materials while working toward the use of conflict-free minerals in our devices. One of our objectives is to ensure that we do not harm communities through an inadvertent <I>de facto</I> embargo of minerals from the Democratic Republic of the Congo
(&#147;DRC&#148;) or an adjoining country (defined as a country that shares an internationally recognized border with the DRC) - both considered a &#147;Covered Country&#148; under the Rule. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">This year&#146;s CMR demonstrates continued improvement and meaningful progress for the 2016 reporting year. The number of
<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Conflict-Free Smelter Program</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> (&#147;CFSP&#148;) compliant smelters or refiners (the
&#147;SORs&#148;) in our supply chain increased from 213 to 249 due to targeted supplier outreach and maturation of the CFSP - of which Microsoft is a founding partner and strong supporter. Based on Microsoft&#146;s data analysis, we also concluded
that 100% of tantalum smelters identified in Microsoft&#146;s supply chain were CFSP compliant. Our 2016 supplier response rate continued to improve and reached 99% during this reporting period (See Figure 1, p. 8). </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Since our last CMR filing, we have also acted to improve our conflict minerals due diligence, including the following: </P>
<P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:10%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Please note: this CMR contains references and hyper-text links to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-Microsoft,</FONT> external websites. These links are provided for informational purposes only. Their inclusion in
this CMR does not establish Microsoft&#146;s endorsement of or assumption of liability for content posted on these external websites. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">1 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Completed implementation of third-party audit firm recommendations covering 2015 reporting year assessment; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Implemented process improvements to increase supplier response rate, including leveraging sourcing manager&#146;s ownership of the supplier response rate, supplier resource support, and tailored outreach to both new
suppliers and previously unresponsive suppliers; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Completed integration of RSRM policy into Microsoft&#146;s Social and Environmental Accountability (&#147;SEA&#148;) audit process to ensure RSRM policy is embedded in suppliers&#146; business processes, particularly in
sourcing and quality management systems; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Refined internal controls and procedures to improve <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> supplier determination, data collection and validation, and supply chain due diligence such as early engagement with
suppliers during <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-boarding</FONT> through Microsoft&#146;s SEA online Audit Management System; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Expanded our supplier engagement by continuously collecting supplier data throughout the year and training suppliers on our RSRM policy to proactively identify and mitigate potential sourcing risk from an unvalidated
SOR with minerals from a Conflict-Affected and High-Risk Area (&#147;CAHRA&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft devices contain one or more 3TGs and are within the
Rule&#146;s scope. Devices manufactured during the 2016 reporting year included: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Surface line of computers and accessories; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Xbox gaming/entertainment consoles and accessories; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Personal computing accessories (mice, headsets and keyboards). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">On the basis of our &#147;Reasonable Country of Origin
Inquiry&#148; (&#147;RCOI&#148;) (see Section II), we cannot exclude the possibility that 3TGs contained in our devices may have originated in a Covered Country. Therefore, we are submitting this CMR, which describes the conflict minerals due
diligence we performed during the 2016 reporting year, as an exhibit to our Form SD. We have published the CMR externally on our corporate website: see <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Responsible Sourcing</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> under the &#147;Raw materials&#148; tab. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The manufacture of devices during any specified time period may include raw materials
sourced before, as well as during, that time period. In particular, some 3TGs used during the 2016 reporting year may have been smelted and refined prior to January&nbsp;31, 2013 and were outside the supply chain prior to the Rule&#146;s initial
reporting period. While such 3TGs are excluded from the Rule&#146;s scope, our RCOI and supply chain due diligence conducted for the 2016 reporting year may have included such minerals. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">2 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>II.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>REASONABLE COUNTRY OF ORIGIN INQUIRY </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Our RCOI corresponds to the first and second steps of the five-step <FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>OECD Due Diligence Guidance for Responsible Supply Chains of Minerals from Conflict-Affected and High-Risk Areas</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;OECD Guidance&#148;) as that Guidance
(including its Supplements) applies to each of the 3TGs and to Microsoft as a &#147;downstream company.&#148; The OECD Guidance provides a framework for detailed due diligence to support responsible global supply chain management of minerals and is
currently the only internationally recognized framework for raw material due diligence. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft does not source directly from 3TG raw material providers.
We source products from suppliers, which source materials, components, and products from their <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-tier</FONT> suppliers. Our supply chain is extensive and complex with many layers of suppliers positioned between
ourselves and 3TG SORs. We refer collectively in this CMR to Microsoft owned manufacturing facilities, directly contracted manufacturing partners, and our strategic component suppliers as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;in-scope</FONT>
suppliers.&#148; Due to our extended supply chain, we leverage our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers to provide information on the sources and chains of custody of 3TGs necessary to the manufacture of our devices. We provide
more detail on our supply chain due diligence process in Section III. The graphic below demonstrates Microsoft&#146;s span of influence with its suppliers. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g405624g0527141609925.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>A.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Establish Strong Company Management Systems </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Company Policies </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft&#146;s RSRM policy describes our commitment and strategy to responsibly source raw
materials used in our devices. Microsoft is committed to the sourcing of raw materials in a way that supports human rights, labor, health and safety, environment, and ethics. This commitment extends to the harvesting, extraction, and transportation
of raw materials globally and to all substances used in our devices - unbounded by specific materials or locations. Our policy supports our implementation of programs that are region-specific and work toward the use of conflict-free minerals in our
devices. We expect our suppliers to support our commitment to the responsible sourcing of raw materials. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The
<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Microsoft Global Human Rights Statement</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> and </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Supplier Code of Conduct</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> defines our expectations concerning ethical business, employment, environmental, and worker safety practices. Our </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Standards of Business Conduct</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> outlines expected behaviors for all Microsoft employees. Our supplier specifications and internal procedures establish supplier commitments for the responsible sourcing of raw materials, including 3TGs. We incorporate
these requirements into our hardware and packaging contracts and audit our suppliers to ensure these requirements are met. </FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt"><FONT COLOR="#FFFFFF">The Microsoft Span of Influence </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">3 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>2.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Internal Management Team </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">A cross-functional team supports Microsoft&#146;s responsible sourcing and 3TG
compliance activities. The Corporate Vice President of Microsoft&#146;s Manufacturing and Supply Chain organization sponsors the team. The team consists of representatives from Sourcing, Social and Environmental Accountability, Manufacturing,
Accounting/Finance, Internal Audit, Windows and Devices Group, Corporate, External and Legal Affairs, Business and Corporate Responsibility, Information Services, and Product Environmental Compliance. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">This team meets quarterly to assess the program&#146;s progress and identify steps necessary to meet our compliance obligations. The team also trains other internal
stakeholders on their roles and responsibilities for implementing and supporting Microsoft&#146;s responsible sourcing program. Related procedures are documented in our internal Responsible Sourcing Program Manual. Team members also develop, review,
file, and publish the CMR. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>3.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>System of Supply Chain Controls and Transparency </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Our Suppliers provide us with information concerning the source
and chain of custody of 3TGs contained in the products and components they supply to us. Many of our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers are also subject to the Rule. These suppliers rely on information provided by their
upstream suppliers to meet their compliance obligations. Our contracts require all Microsoft <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers partners to identify by weight each and every substance contained in the materials, components,
and products supplied to us, including 3TGs. Our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers are responsible for communicating our sourcing requirements and specifications to their <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-tier</FONT>
suppliers and incorporating 3TG information from their <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-tier</FONT> suppliers. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">In addition, we require all <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers to submit a Conflict Minerals Reporting Template (&#147;CMRT&#148;) annually. These CMRTs are evaluated for completeness, data integrity, due diligence thoroughness, and sourcing risk. Potential
risks may include a failure to fully complete the CMRT, data inconsistencies, and possible sourcing from a CAHRA. Microsoft investigates each identified issue and engages with those suppliers to address all concerns in conformance to Microsoft
policies, procedures, and specifications. In cases where the supplier is identified as sourcing from a CAHRA, suppliers are required to submit a CMRT more frequently. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">If we find that a supplier has introduced unmitigated risk to the Microsoft supply chain, such as using an upstream SOR that does not comply with Microsoft&#146;s RSRM
policy or specifications, Microsoft requires corrective action to address the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-conformity.</FONT> The response time for corrective action is calibrated to the severity of the identified risk. Risks are mitigated
by supplier engagement, corrective actions, training, and/or additional audits. These controls and related documentation are detailed in H02050 - Microsoft Supplier Social and Environmental Accountability Manual and other Microsoft internal
operating procedures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft works with impacted suppliers to find sources for compliant minerals. If a supplier does not commit to an alternate source within a
reasonable time period, Microsoft places the supplier on restricted status with no new Microsoft business awarded until the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-conformance</FONT> is resolved. Microsoft may also terminate its business relationship
with the supplier. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">4 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft is a longstanding member of the <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Global <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-Sustainability</FONT> Initiative</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;GeSI&#148;) and the </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Electronics Industry Citizenship Coalition</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;EICC&#148;). These organizations initiated the </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Conflict-Free Sourcing Initiative</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;CFSI&#148;) in 2008. The
CFSI is one of the most utilized and respected resources for addressing supply chain conflict minerals issues. The CFSI, through its CFSP, uses an independent third-party audit to monitor whether SORs process 3TGs from sources that directly or
indirectly finance or benefit armed groups in a Covered Country. Microsoft funded an early adopters program to subsidize audit costs, enabling more SORs to be CFSP audited. Microsoft also financially supports the </FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Industrial Technology Research Institute&#146;s Tin Supply Chain Initiative</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;iTSCi&#148;), which has established a system of traceability and due diligence
in Covered Countries. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft works to positively impact <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-to-end</FONT></FONT> mining
sustainability, from artisanal mines to larger mining enterprises. Through this work, we aspire to improve conditions directly at the source across a broad scope of issues in partnership with the electronics industry, the mining industry, and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">not-for-profit</FONT></FONT> partners. We improve practices associated with the mining of metal ores at their source through participation in collaborative initiatives related to the
upstream mining industry. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft supports and participates in numerous partnerships that work to establish responsible mining standards and the responsible
sourcing of minerals. We partner closely with Pact, the Initiative for Responsible Mining Assurance (&#147;IRMA&#148;), and Alliance for Responsible Mining (&#147;ARM&#148;). These organizations address human rights concerns in mining and leverage
data and technology to bring about even greater change. Empowered by digital technology, Microsoft and our partners can drive transformations in the mining sector by addressing issues of increased scope and complexity. We believe this integrated
approach improves conditions for the people working in raw material supply chains. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Our primary relationships are further described below: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Pact</U></FONT>: Since 2014, Microsoft has partnered with Pact on the Watoto Inje ya Mungoti, or &#147;Children out of Mining&#148; program - a scalable, repeatable, and sustainable strategy to
address child labor in the DRC mining sector. The program employs a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-pronged</FONT> approach, focused on raising community awareness of the child labor issue and improving economic stability of caregivers. By
October 2016, Pact reported a 97% reduction in children working in the mines. The program and Microsoft&#146;s leadership have been recognized by others and was the only cited best practice by the OECD in its report, <I>Practical Actions for
Companies to Identify and Address the Worst Forms of Child Labour in the Minerals Supply Chain</I>, presented at the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">OECD-ICGLR-UN</FONT> Group of Expert Forum on Responsible Mineral Supply Chain in May 2016. As the
program expands and develops, Microsoft will continue to partner with Pact with the goal of transforming this initiative into a best practice standard to address child labor in mining. Please find more about the project in Pact&#146;s <FONT
 COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Report</U></FONT>. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Initiative for Responsible Mining Assurance (&#147;IRMA&#148;)</U></FONT>: IRMA established a
multi-stakeholder and independently verifiable responsible mining assurance system that improves social and environmental performance through the development of global mining standards for large-scale mines. Our partnership involves more than just
participation - we are bringing technology to help scope, scale, and implement effective programs. Microsoft recently donated a technology platform to IRMA that will allow the organization to better implement
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">5 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">
these assurance standards. By pairing the technology platform with Power BI, a cloud-based business analytics service, stakeholders will be able to track mining performance against the assurance
standards. This real-time information, presented in an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">easy-to-see</FONT></FONT> and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">easy-to-use</FONT></FONT>
interface, will help mining companies and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Governmental</FONT> Organizations (&#147;NGOs&#148;) overcome the inherent difficulties of scope and complexity of these programs to create new insights and inspire
additional progress. With learnings from this engagement, we hope to enable additional NGO partners to expand their work to create sustainable mining communities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Alliance for Responsible Mining (&#147;ARM&#148;)</U></FONT>: ARM sets standards for responsible artisanal and small scale mining and supports and creates opportunities for gold miners,
providing them with incentives to become responsible economic, technological, and environmental enterprises. Seed funding from Microsoft helped ARM secure further resources to develop a Market Entry Standard for Artisanal and Small-scale Gold
Miners. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>4.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Supplier Engagement </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Given the complexities of the global mineral supply chain, we work closely with our suppliers
around the world to ensure they share our commitment and reflect it in their own programs. CFSI&#146;s &#147;<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Practical Guidance for Downstream
Companies</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">&#148; states that &#147;all of the [OECD Guidance&#146;s] red flag triggers are contained in the upstream portion of the supply chain.&#148; Because these conflict mineral supply chain
&#147;triggers&#148; are directed to upstream companies, rather than downstream manufacturers such as Microsoft, we mitigate 3TG sourcing risks by working with our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers to identify 3TG SORs and
encourage those facilities to become CFSP compliant or, failing to do so, use an alternate facility that is CFSP compliant. We also participate in industry-wide initiatives, such as the CFSP, that assess SOR compliance with the OECD Guidance as
recommended by CFSI guidance. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">We drive responsible sourcing through our extended supply chain by surveying our
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers&#146; sourcing of raw materials in their upstream supply chains. We also use tools that include supplier and smelter capability building and support broader industry efforts to promote
responsible mining and sourcing. Finally, we conduct audits of our contracted suppliers to verify conformance to Microsoft requirements. More information is set forth below. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><U>Supplier Requirements</U>: We require our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers to meet our material disclosure requirements and related responsible sourcing policies through contractual
provisions and product specifications. We communicate, monitor, and track electronically supplier adherance to ensure conformance. These policies and procedures are outlined in Section III. We also train our directly contracted suppliers to meet our
requirements through training sessions, educational forums, and direct communications. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><U>Capability Building and Partnerships</U>: We work closely with our supply chain partners to build the raw material supplier capabilities for achieving our responsible sourcing goals. With the empowerment of digital
technology, Microsoft and our partners can drive transformations in the mining sector by addressing issues of increased scope and complexity. We invest in industry programs, such as the CFSP, to increase suppliers&#146; capabilities and provide them
with platforms to share best practices. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">6 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><U>Supplier Audits</U>: Microsoft conducts audits of its directly contracted suppliers to assess their conformance to Microsoft requirements. All new contracted hardware and packaging suppliers undergo an Initial
Capability Assessment (&#147;ICA&#148;) to verify conformance. Existing contracted hardware and packaging suppliers also undergo a Sustaining Maintenance Audit (&#147;SMA&#148;) on an annual, biannual, or triannual basis depending on their risk
level. Suppliers must establish and maintain a corporate policy and effective procedures for responsible sourcing of raw materials. Microsoft selects and retains only those business partners committed to meeting these requirements. A failure by a
supplier or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-tier</FONT> supplier to conform to these requirements may constitute a breach of the supplier&#146;s contractual agreement with Microsoft. During the 2016 reporting year, Microsoft-engaged auditors
conducted 165 ICAs and SMAs of approximately 320 directly contracted hardware and packaging suppliers to assess areas of SEA conformance. These ICAs and SMAs addressed whether the suppliers had a conflict minerals policy, systems in place to
implement that policy, and documentation to verify conformance to Microsoft&#146;s responsible sourcing requirements. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>5.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Grievance Mechanism </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft&#146;s Global Human Rights Statement expresses our commitment to provide an
anonymous grievance reporting mechanism for our employees and other stakeholders who may be impacted by our operations. Microsoft&#146;s <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>Business Conduct Hotline</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> allows employees and others to anonymously ask compliance questions or report concerns regarding Microsoft&#146;s business operations, including our mineral sourcing policies or those of our suppliers. We investigate and,
where appropriate, take remedial action to address reported concerns. We also participate in industry efforts to develop grievance mechanisms for conflict minerals-related issues. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>B.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Identify and Assess Risk in the Supply Chain </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">We took the following steps to identify and assess supplier conflict
mineral sourcing risk during this reporting year<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Using the Rule and SEC guidance, we generated a list of potential <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers to receive Microsoft&#146;s annual CMRT survey. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">We surveyed all potential <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers to determine the status of any 3TGs contained in devices manufactured during the 2016 reporting year by utilizing the CFSI-standard
CMRT and the services of a third-party solution provider. The survey followed OECD Guidance as tailored for Microsoft&#146;s role as a downstream company. Our survey included questions regarding the supplier&#146;s 3TG due diligence policies and
procedures, its practices for engaging with its upstream suppliers, a request to list all SORs from which its 3TGs were sourced, and other detailed questions concerning the origins of 3TGs contained in the supplier&#146;s products.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:10%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Microsoft completed its supplier conflict mineral sourcing data analysis for the 2016 reporting year on March&nbsp;31, 2017. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">7 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">We reviewed all supplier CMRT submissions to validate that they were complete and to identify any contradictions or inconsistencies. We worked with our third-party solution provider to secure updated responses from
suppliers, as needed. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">We identified 252 active <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers for the 2016 reporting year. Of the 252 active in-scope suppliers surveyed, we received responses from 251 by our March 31<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">st</SUP> deadline. This resulted in a 99% response rate - an improvement from previous years as shown in Figure 1. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Figure 1. Response Rate for Active <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">In-scope</FONT> Suppliers (2013-2016 Reporting Years) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g405624g0527141610128.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>III.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>DUE DILIGENCE DESIGN AND PERFORMANCE </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">On the basis of our RCOI, we determined that 3TGs contained in our devices
may have originated in one or more Covered Country. Accordingly, we designed and performed due diligence on the source and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">chain-of-custody</FONT></FONT> of those 3TGs. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>A.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Due Diligence Design </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Our 3TG due diligence process conforms to the third and fourth steps of the five-step OECD
Guidance. The first and second steps of the five-step OECD Guidance were addressed in Section II. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">8 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>B.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Due Diligence Performed </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Design and Implement a Strategy to Respond to Risks </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft requires its suppliers to minimize the possible
sourcing of 3TGs from CAHRAs through contract requirements incorporating supplier specifications. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="13%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>a.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Microsoft Supplier Specifications - H00594 and HO0642 </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft requires 100% identification of all materials,
including 3TGs, used in packaging and hardware products and parts on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">component-by-component</FONT></FONT> level through supplier specification H00594, Restricted Substances for
Hardware Products. H00594 requires contracted suppliers to: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Post a responsible sourcing policy, conforming to the OECD Guidance, on their website; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Exercise due diligence on the source and chain of custody of 3TGs contained in materials, components, or products supplied to Microsoft; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Identify, by name, each SOR that has processed or otherwise handled 3TGs contained in those materials, components, or products; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Encourage those SORs to participate in available CFSP or an equivalent third-party conflict-free audit scheme; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Confirm 3TGs in their supply chain are sourced from available SORs that are compliant with the CFSP or an equivalent independent private sector audit firm; and </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Notify Microsoft immediately if minerals used in the supplied materials, components, or products may contain 3TGs sourced from a Covered Country. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">H00594 requires Microsoft suppliers to impose these same requirements on their <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-tier</FONT> suppliers and to assist <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-tier</FONT> suppliers with appropriate training and support. To facilitate this process, H00642, Restricted Substances Control System for Hardware Products, requires Microsoft suppliers to utilize the CMRT provided by
the CFSI and available at <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#1e5eff"><U>www.conflictfreesourcing.org</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. Suppliers must submit an annual CMRT and updated data upon request or when sourcing practices
change. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="13%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>b.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Responsible Sourcing Program Manual Processes to Implement OECD Guidance </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft uses OECD Guidance to review
supplier CMRT data and identify potential red flags for the sourcing of 3TGs. We take additional action when indentifying red flags such as: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The minerals originated from or were transported via a CAHRA; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The minerals were claimed to have originated from a country that has limited known reserves for the mineral in question; </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">9 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The minerals were claimed to have originated from a country in which minerals from a CAHRA are known to transit; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The company&#146;s suppliers or other known upstream companies have shareholder or other interests in companies that supply minerals or operate in one of the red flag locations of mineral origin and transit; and
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The company&#146;s suppliers or other known upstream companies were known to have sourced minerals from a red flag location of mineral origin and transit in the last 12 months. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft&#146;s program includes an escalation process that requires an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> supplier to find an alternative to a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-CFSP</FONT> compliant source of 3TGs for use in materials, components, or products supplied to Microsoft or risk termination as a Microsoft supplier. To date, we have not encountered a RSRM issue with a supplier that
has warranted contract termination. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft&#146;s internal Responsible Sourcing Program Manual requires self-assessment, monitoring, and internal reporting of
the RSRM program progress and compliance. The internal management team provided monthly program status updates, including metrics and audit results, to Microsoft&#146;s Corporate Vice President of Manufacturing and Supply Chain. We utilized supplier
survey updates, supplier communications, supplier social and environmental accountability audits, and new supplier briefings to prevent the introduction of any new 3TG sourcing risk to our supply chain. We leveraged Microsoft&#146;s SEA Steering
Committee meetings with senior management to report findings and receive program guidance. Microsoft employees accessed the results of the program through Microsoft&#146;s Windows and Devices Group&#146;s internal 2016 Sustainability Report. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="13%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>c.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Industry and Partner Engagement </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft participated in or has been a member of several industry-wide
responsible mining and smelting initiatives: CFSI, ITRI&#146;s iTSCi program, IRMA, Pact, and ARM. We also conducted smelter outreach on behalf of the CFSI Smelter Engagement Team to further the CFSI program. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>2.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Carried Out Independent Third-Party Audit of Supply Chain Due Diligence </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">As contemplated by OECD Guidance, our due
diligence program leveraged independent SOR audits. The audits complied with the CFSP and other similar programs. Microsoft obtained SOR data from the CFSP Compliant Smelter List using <I>Reasonable Country of Origin Inquiry Data</I> for member
<I>MSFT</I>. The list identifies SORs that have undergone assessment through the CFSP or industry equivalent program, such as Responsible Jewellery Council (&#147;RJC&#148;) or London Bullion Market Association (&#147;LBMA&#148;). We used the list
to support certain statements contained in this CMR. Microsoft also participated in CFSI&#146;s Smelter Engagement Team during the 2016 reporting year. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">10 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>3.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Reported on Supply Chain Due Diligence </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft&#146;s RSRM policy and other responsible sourcing documents are
available on our external website. We have filed our CMR with the SEC and concurrently posted it on our external Responsible Sourcing website. These disclosures meet the fifth step of the OECD Guidance. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>IV.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>SOR INFORMATION </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>A.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>3TG Processing Facilities </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft has made a reasonable good faith effort to collect and evaluate information
concerning 3TG SORs provided by our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers. The vast majority of our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers provided data at a company or divisional level. This level of
disclosure was expected given the multiple tiers of supply chain actors positioned between our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-scope</FONT> suppliers and 3TG SORs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Our supplier survey data revealed 17,823 potential 3TG SORs in the Microsoft supply chain. We validated the data by removing duplicate SORs, reconciling multiple SOR
names for a single entity, and eliminating otherwise invalid SOR names. We then verified if the alleged smelters were active and participants in the CFSP audit program. We determined 303 smelters met this criteria. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Figures below provide a visual depiction of the SORs identified in Microsoft&#146;s supply chain by CFSP audit status. Figure 2 categorizes the SORs by CFSP audit
status and reporting year. Figure 2 indicates the percentage of compliant or CFSP active smelters has steadily increased each year. For the 2016 reporting year, 87% of suppliers were either compliant or on the CFSP active list. This is an increase
from 85% in 2015, 73% in 2014 and 60% in 2013. Figure 2 also indicates that the number of compliant smelters increased significantly from 213 to 249. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Figure 3
categorizes the SORs by 3TG mineral and CFSP audit status. A comparison from the 2015 reporting year showed that gold, tungsten, and tin all increased in the number and percentage of Compliant and Active smelters. Tin had the greatest increase with
the percentage of Compliant or Active smelters growing from 85% to 91%. Gold and tungsten had moderate increases while tantalum remained 100% compliant. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>C.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>3TG Mines or Locations of Origin </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft obtained Reasonable Country of Origin data through our
membership in the CFSI using the <I>Reasonable Country of Origin Inquiry Data</I> for member <I>MSFT</I>. We used this data to determine the 3TG country of origin of SORs identified in Microsoft&#146;s supply chain. Microsoft supports the continued
refinement and expansion of the list of participating SORs in the CFSP audit program through our membership in CFSI. The CFSI oversees the CFSP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">We
encouraged SORs to participate in the CFSP by contacting all <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-compliant</FONT> SORs identified in our supply chain each reporting year. We also required suppliers reporting
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-compliant</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:10%">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">
SORs to contact these SORs and motivate them to join the CFSP. We actively supported outreach events to increase CFSP SOR coverage. We funded a third party to help educate SORs and prepare them
for the audit process. We have also offered to visit SORs to facilitate their participation in the CFSP. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>V.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>IMPROVEMENTS </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">This year&#146;s report documents our efforts to expand the number of verified conflict-free SORs in
our supply chain and demonstrates strong progress. While comparisons to 2015 reporting year data are not precise due to supply chain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> variances, the progress
is meaningful. Microsoft&#146;s key 2016 reporting year accomplishments and improvements are detailed below: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Increased number of CFSP-compliant SORs identified in Microsoft&#146;s supply chain from 213 to 249 due to enhanced supplier outreach, and maturation of CFSI&#146;s CFSP; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Increased supplier response rate to 99% in the 2016 reporting year - an increase from 71% in 2013; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Enhanced engagement with external organizations, such as Pact, IRMA, and ARM that are committed to advancing responsible sourcing on a global basis by developing mining standards and addressing issues such as child
labor in the mining industry. We partner closely with these organizations and leverage data and technology to bring about even greater change. With the further empowerment that digital technology can provide toward increased scope and complexity,
Microsoft and our partners can drive positive transformations in the mining sector. We believe this integrated approach is the most effective way to improve conditions for the people working in raw material supply chains; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Refined and improved internal procedures and processes to enhance alignment with OECD Guidance, including Microsoft&#146;s supplier escalation process and supplier audit procedures; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Increased Microsoft&#146;s level of engagement with suppliers and internal stakeholders by holding supplier forums, webinars, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> trainings, and by providing resources;
and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Continued refinement of supplier data by conducting outreach when reported data was incomplete or uncertain. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>VI.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>FUTURE ACTIONS </B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft is committed to human rights, labor, health and safety, environmental protection, and
business ethics in our supply chain. We will advance implementation of our RSRM policy. The policy consists of supply chain identification and risk assessment, standardized requirements and verification, capability building, transparency, and
partnerships. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">We will continue encouraging SORs to participate in the CFSP and expanding our knowledge about 3TGs in our supply chain. Our ability to identify,
assess, and mitigate risks associated with our raw materials sourcing will improve with ongoing due diligence efforts - both direct and with our </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">20 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">
partners. Consistent with our commitments, we intend to take the following steps to improve our responsible sourcing of raw materials due diligence efforts:</P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Enhance our use of digital technology to improve supply chain information and risk mitigation; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
